   }
   ai_weight = {
      weight = 1000
   }
}

### Marine Detachment - Marine detachment 
utility_component_template = {
   key = "required_aura_cruiser_marines_1"
   size = medium
   icon = "GFX_ship_part_required_aura_cruiser_marines_1"
   icon_frame = 1
   power = -100
   resources = {
      category = ship_components
      cost = { alloys = 80 }
      upkeep = { alloys = 0.16 energy = 0.64 }   }
   prerequisites = { tech_society_marines_1 }
   component_set = "required_aura_cruiser"
   upgrades_to = required_aura_cruiser_marines_2
   size_restriction = { sovereign exploration_cruiser }

   scripted_action_possible = {
	   is_colony = yes
      exists = owner
      owner = { is_same_value = prev.from.owner }
      OR = {
         has_planet_flag = "deliver_security_from:@from"
         NOT = { has_planet_flag = "deliver_security" }
      }
	}
	scripted_action_button_possible = {
      custom_tooltip = {
         fail_text = "requires_owned_system"
         exists = space_owner
         space_owner = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
      }
	}

	scripted_action_finished = { has_planet_flag = "deliver_security_finished" }
	scripted_action_name = on_assist_deliver_security_reached
	scripted_action_tooltip = deliver_security_ship_button
	scripted_action_icon = GFX_fleet_order_button_deliver_security_action
	scripted_action_on_cancel = on_deliver_security_action_cancel
	scripted_action_activity_key = assist_security_action_activity_key
   scripted_action_context_menu_name = assist_security_context_menu_title


   hostile_aura = {
      name = "aura_marines"
      radius = 1
      apply_on = ships
      stack_info = { id = hostile_marine_aura priority = 1 }
   }
   ai_weight = {
      weight = 100
      modifier = {
         factor = 0.0
         resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value < 100 }
      }
   }
}

   key = "required_aura_cruiser_bio_damage"
   size = medium
   icon = "GFX_ship_part_required_aura_cruiser_bio_damage"
   icon_frame = 1
   power = -140
   resources = {
      category = ship_components
      cost = { sr_crew = 120 }
      upkeep = { sr_crew = 0.24 energy = 0.96 }   }
   prerequisites = { tech_undine_coordination }
   component_set = "required_aura_cruiser"
   size_restriction = { undine_01_bio_cruiser }
   friendly_aura = {
      name = "aura_bio_damage"
      radius = 50
      apply_on = ships
      stack_info = { id = friendly_support_aura priority = 200 }
      modifier = { ship_weapon_damage = 0.1 ship_tracking_add = 5 ship_accuracy_add = 5   }
   }
   ai_weight = {
      weight = 10
      modifier = {
         factor = 0.0
         resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value < 100 }
      }
   }
}

   }
}
